< Text>
This is a remote destination for travelers on interstate 5 and they have a sign clearly posted on the door with the insidiously gleeful message "restroom for customers only, your purchase is your key". If this was an inner city location to curb camping or something like that I would understand but to intentionally deny a restroom when you are already making heaps of $ just to ensure every person entering the establishment is a customer. They ought to be ashamed of themselves. I turned around as soon as I read the sign.</Text>

< Review>
Busy place as it is at a major freeway exchange.
I found this place to be clean and we'll stocked of goods and gas prices reasonable.
When I paid for my goods and gas at the counter I was greeted by the most friendly hostess that gave me some helpful advice on my purchases.
At the pumps the window washing stations were we'll stocked with towels and clean washing liquid.
This was a very pleasant visit and I will most certainly stop here again.</Review>

<response>None<//response><username>Julia Babka-Kurzrock</username><Rate>5<//Rate>< Text>
Cliffs are showing their age, attempts to buttress them are failing and some houses seem in danger of becoming part of the beach. There are several damaged staircases that are not in use, so watch the tide and plan your trip if you're going along the shore.  You have to find the working, stable staircases to get back up to the street. The rocks, boulders, barnacles, algae and shells are nice to examine for contrast while you're exploring the beach. Lots of surfers and dogs on the beach.<//Text>

I wasn't looking for a car but then while at the stop light I saw a mean looking Mustang on their front line glaring at me. I was interested. Around 4 days later on the way back from the Farmers Market I took my husband by to see the car.  We looked at it and Sebastian came out to see if we needed help. We talked a little and told him we were just looking at it since we had groceries in the car. He did not use high pressure tactics and was just nice and informative. He did give us his card. I decided that I really wanted the car so I did my due diligence. I looked online, found out information on it, went to other lots but I liked this Mustang (it was specially ordered by the owner so it was not just stock). I was buying out my leased Ford Mustang and this was the last stop after contacting Ford. I had been to three other dealerships in the area and the experience wasn't so great. One of the dealerships openly told me that they can't sell a leased car because they do not make money on it. The other two were very shady when it came to questions.

However, things were different at Ford Ventura, they reached out to me and helped me schedule an appointment. The process was quick, clear and very comfortable. I rated 4 starts and not 5 because I still don't agree that I will have to have a ford credit inquiry on my account although I have a pre-approved loan.

< Text>
I have been twice and both times have not been happy with my food. The first time the filling for the crepes was watery, bland and grainy. I thought I would give it another try and ordered a Belgan waffle, thinking that you could not go wrong with such a simple thing. But the waffle was so tough it was difficult to cut and chew. It felt like it had been sitting in a warmer for several hours. The butter that was served with it was hard and would not spread and the syrup was served in a tiny container that was half full. There was not nearly enough and my waffle was tough, dry and with hard clumps of butter. I also ordered a side of hashbrowns that were nice and crispy, the way I like it, but had a seasoning on top that was way over done. It was so salty I could not even enjoy them. In addition, the only decent place to sit is outside, due to the noise level inside, but there are so many flies and yellow jackets that it makes it most unpleasant. It is a cute place, but the servers are so overwhelmed that you have to constantly ask for things, which never end up being brought to you, or come so far after the fact you no longer need it. I am sad to say I won’t be returning.< /Text>

<username>Allison Hansen< /username><time>1540084906980</time><Rating>5< /Rating>< Review>
Dungeness crab. In Paradise. Go there. New owners have done a fabulous redesign - farmhouse kitchen - a fresh look on an old timey theme, and have added decking and additional outdoor seating. It is comfortable and light and airy and exceedingly clean.
The food, goodness it is good. It is Great. Best clam chowder north of the Bay area, and a tomato soup so full of flavor it is like a little harvest in a bowl.
There are several delicious and unique Eggs Benedict dishes to choose from, but I am stuck on the sheer novelty of being able to order Dungeness crab right here in Paradise. They feature it both a Benedict and an Omelet. Go there. Best breakfast on the ridge.< /Review>

< Text>
Came here after a bad experience somewhere else and I'm glad I did. Came in Thursday at 7 and it was not packed but lively. The waitresses were very friendly, they let us vent about the bad service elsewhere, recommended plates for us to eat and did it all with a smile. Not to mention the selection of beer was very tasty. The food was delicious and unique. We got the sampler platter and the pizza on a tortilla (can't remember the name) and enjoyed every bite. It looks like this place probably gets crowded on the weekends but it is a sports bar so that's to be expected. Big TV's and dim lighting make it a nice hang out spot.<//Text>

< review>
Best sports bar I've been too. Great service and the food at night is delicious</review>
<date>1511740783008< /date>< Pics>
None<//Pics>
<gmapID>0x80c2b69fa0e8881d:0x7b20bbcbb71d9d8e< /gmapID></record></dataset><record>
<Time>1447352602495< /Time>< gmap_id>
0x80c2b69fa0e8881d:0x7b20bbcbb71d9d8e</gmap_id>
< rate>
5</rate>
<pictures>None</pictures>< review>
Finally made it to this sports bar after driving by all the time on my way to the gym. I had no idea how it would look inside and to my surprise it was very nice! The decor is perfect. They have plenty of TVs all around for your sports enjoyment. It isn't very big, but it feels like you're at a sporting event. Loud, laughter, cheering, booing, etc., is all you here while you're there until the games are over and it gets quieter.
The day I went was very full, Dodger playoff game, UCLA Football and NFL were all on at the same time. We waited a little, but were seated in a waiting area and were allowed to order drinks while they found my friend and I a seat. It took about 10 minutes and we were sat in the mix of all the rukkus.
The selection of beers is great. Plenty to choose from whatever your liking may be. They did run out of one that I was interested in. Shows how popular it is. The food menu all looked delicious. I ended up ordering a chicken quesadilla, and my friend ordered chicken tacos. We both shared guacamole and chips. All of it was delicious!!!! The chicken was marinated perfectly. The presentation of the food was also really great.
Needless to say, I will be back at Flights to watch more sports and try out other items on their menu. Their wings and nachos looked so yummy but I was too stuffed to have more. Great service and plenty of parking!</review>

<Rate>5</Rate><Gmap_id>0x80c2b69fa0e8881d:0x7b20bbcbb71d9d8e</Gmap_id><name>Terry Walker< /name><user_id>109138202419714805075< /user_id><Resp>None</Resp>< text>
We came here to watch Sunday night football, have a few beers and get a bite to eat. Service was great. Very friendly staff. Beer and wine only, no cocktails. Typical bar menu (wings, burgers and nachos) but food was tasty. We had the Propeller nachos and it was almost more than the 2 of us could eat!  Prices are reasonable. There are no bad seats in the house. Parking is a bit tight, so get here early on game day. I should mention that this was our second attempt, Saturday was "fight night" and even though we showed up at 4pm to watch the Notre Dame game, our seats would have cost us $20 a piece at 5:30 to stick around for the second half. We opted to find somewhere else to watch the game. Check the schedule before you go.<//text>
